I'm very happy to see this article. It was mentioned on Twitter, which is
where I first saw it.

H3ABionet (http://www.h3abionet.org/) recently ran a containers and
workflows hackathon. The two workflow systems used were Nextflow and the
Common Workflow Language (CWL). The two systems were chosen, in part,
because they both have very responsive communities. Great to hear that
Nextflow gets interest in Singularity, and Alain Dommisey is looking into
CWL and  Singularity.

Good things are happening!

Peter

PS I'm sure 2017 will see the adoption of Singularity on the South African
CHPC Lengau cluster. We're nearly there.
